   65 | t161 = GET:I32(cc_ndep)
   66 | t162 = armg_calculate_condition(t157,t159,t160,t161):Ity_I32
   67 | t163 = 32to1(t162)
   68 | if (t163) { PUT(pc) = 0x40006d; Ijk_Boring }
   NEXT: PUT(pc) = 0x00400307; Ijk_Boring
}
